[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         A Jazzer fuzzing run triggered a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` exception indicating [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         a file path traversal vulnerability. The sanitizer detected that an                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         archive-expanding routine attempted to write or move files outside of an intended   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         directory, causing the fuzzer harness [1m([0m`ExpanderFuzzer`[1m)[0m to crash when invoking     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `Expander.expand`.                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Issue                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           A `com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` exception was    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         raised with the message “File path traversal:                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/tmp/expander-tmp7422229540301078632/output/q/r/[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m”. This indicates   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         that during archive extraction, at least one file entry contained a path that would [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         escape the designated output directory.                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Vulnerability Type                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           File path traversal: an adversarial archive entry uses relative path components   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0me.g., `..[35m/[0m`[1m)[0m or absolute paths to write files outside of the intended extraction   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         directory.                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Key Observations                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The exception originates in `FilePathTraversal.check` [1m([0mline [1;36m346[0m[1m)[0m and propagates [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         through `checkPath` and `copyMismatchMvHook` in the same sanitizer class.           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The sanitizer is invoked by                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander.expand`, across several    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         overloads [1m([0mlines [1;36m216[0m, [1;36m336[0m, [1;36m412[0m, [1;36m502[0m[1m)[0m.                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The fuzzer entry point is `ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput` [1m([0mline [1;36m52[0m[1m)[0m, which  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         feeds arbitrary input to the `Expander` utility.                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The sanitizer correctly identifies and halts on disallowed file paths before    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         actual file system writes complete.                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Relevant Code Areas for Investigation                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • `com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.FilePathTraversal` – logic for         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         detecting and blocking path traversal.                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • `org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander` – handling of archive [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         entries, path normalization, and file writing/moving.                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • `ExpanderFuzzer` harness – how inputs are passed and whether path validation or [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         sandboxing is applied prior to invoking `Expander`.                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtargetDirectory.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mzae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m492[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mtarget.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirectory[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m493[0m[39m:                    throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mString.format[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Zip slip '%s' + '%s' [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m-> '%s'"[0m[39m,[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m494[0m[39m:                            targetDirectory, [0m[1;35mzae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, target[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m495[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m496[0m[39m:                Path parent = [0m[1;35mcreateParentDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirectory, target[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m497[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m! [0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m498[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;35mparent.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m499[0m[39m:                    target = [0m[1;35mparent.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtarget.getFileName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m500[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m501[0m[39m:                try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream is = [0m[1;35marchive.getInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mzae[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m502[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;35mFiles.copy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, target[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m503[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Locate the generic `expand` method in `Expander.java`.**  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   File: [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/examples/Expander.java`, lines[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m~[0m[1;36m68[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m94[0m[39m.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Introduce a path‐prefix check immediately after resolving & normalizing each [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentry’s target path.**  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After line [0m[1;36m74[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`final Path targetPath = …`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, insert:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Prevent file‐path traversal [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmirror “zip slip” guard[0m[1;39m)[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     Path normalizedTarget = [0m[1;35mtargetPath.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mnormalizedTarget.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mString.format[0m[1;39m([0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[32m"File path traversal: '%s' -> '%s'"[0m[39m,[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             targetDirPath, normalizedTarget[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace all subsequent uses of `targetPath` in this loop with [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`normalizedTarget`.  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - For directory entries [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mnextEntry.isDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, use `normalizedTarget` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhen creating directories.  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - For file entries, compute the parent via `[0m[1;35mnormalizedTarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcreate it if needed, and write to `normalizedTarget`.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Rationale and details**  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Why:** The generic `expand` method currently delegates to [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mnextEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` but never verifies that the resolved path [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremains under the intended extraction directory. Malicious archive entries with [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`..[0m[35m/[0m[39m` or absolute paths can escape, triggering the Jazzer path‐traversal sanitizer.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBy mirroring the ZIP‐specific [0m[32m"zip slip"[0m[39m guard [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m490[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m493[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, we close this [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mloophole for all formats.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Preserves existing logic:**  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Valid entries inside `targetDirPath` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mincluding those creating [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msubdirectories[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will normalize to a path that still starts with [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`targetDirPath`—they pass the check and fall through to the existing [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectory-[0m[35m/[0m[95mfile[0m[39m‐creation logic unchanged [0m[1;39m([0m[39maside from using the normalized path[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Entries attempting to escape will be caught early, raising an `IOException` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore any file system writes, satisfying both security requirements and harness [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexpectations.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Consistency:**  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Uses the same `[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` + `[0m[1;35mstartsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` pattern already proven in the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mZIP‐specific code path, ensuring uniform protection across all archive types [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandled by `expand`.  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Side effects & mitigation:**  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Some valid entries with tricky constructs [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `foo/.[0m[35m/[0m[95mbar[0m[39m` or redundant [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mseparators[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will normalize harmlessly.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Absolute‐path entries will normalize to root‐based paths, failing the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpredicate and being rejected.  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - No change to harness code, external libraries, or tests—only the core [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Expander` logic is tightened.  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Verification steps**  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run existing unit/integration tests for `Expander` to confirm no regressions [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min valid archive extraction.  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add a minimal fuzz harness test or unit test that tries to extract an entry [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnamed `..[0m[35m/[0m[95mevil.txt[0m[39m` in a non‐ZIP format; assert that it throws `IOException` with [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mour “File path traversal” message.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Re‐run Jazzer to confirm that the previous `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` crash[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis replaced by a controlled exception from the `Expander` code, and that the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mharness does not crash unexpectedly.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNo modifications to harness or test code are required—this single insertion fully [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maddresses the path traversal vulnerability in the generic archive‐expander path.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         The initial issue arises when the fuzzer triggers a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical`   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         exception from Jazzer’s `FilePathTraversal` sanitizer during archive expansion in   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `Expander.expand`. The sanitizer flags an extracted entry whose resolved path       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         escapes the intended target directory. A patch was applied to normalize the         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         resolved path, verify it still starts with the target directory, and throw an       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `IOException` on failure. After applying the patch, the sanitizer still reports a   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         file path traversal violation at a slightly shifted line number, indicating that    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         the added check did not fully address all traversal cases in the codebase.          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Initial Issue                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The fuzzer invokes `Expander.expand`, which iterates over archive entries and     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         writes them to disk.                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - During this process, the sanitizer detects that an entry’s resolved path          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0m`[1;35mnextEntry.resolveIn[0m[1m([0mtargetDirPath[1m)[0m`[1m)[0m can escape the `targetDirPath`, triggering:  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: File path           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         traversal: [35m/tmp/.../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           at `FilePathTraversal.check` → `checkPath` → `copyMismatchMvHook` →               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m`.                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - This indicates an exploitable path traversal: malicious archive entries can       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         overwrite or create files outside the intended directory.                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Important Observations                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The exception is raised by Jazzer’s sanitizer, not by application logic.          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The crash occurs before any file I/O succeeds, during the path-resolution phase.  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The harness [1m([0m`ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[1m)[0m only drives the code under      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         test; it is not the root cause.                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Patch Attempt                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m. In `Expander.java`, around line [1;36m71[0m [1m([0min the loop over entries[1m)[0m, the single-line   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         resolution                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            `final Path targetPath = nullTarget ? null :                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mnextEntry.resolveIn[0m[1m([0mtargetDirPath[1m)[0m;`                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            is replaced with:                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            ```                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            final Path rawTargetPath = nullTarget ? null :                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mnextEntry.resolveIn[0m[1m([0mtargetDirPath[1m)[0m;                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            Path targetPath = rawTargetPath;                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            if [1m([0m!nullTarget[1m)[0m [1m{[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                Path normalized = [1;35mrawTargetPath.normalize[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m;                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                if [1m([0m![1;35mnormalized.startsWith[0m[1m([0mtargetDirPath[1m)[0m[1m)[0m [1m{[0m                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m            [1m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m. This adds an explicit check that the normalized resolved path does not escape    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         the target directory.                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m. Subsequent code for directories and file extraction remains unchanged.           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m501[0m[39m:                try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream is = [0m[1;35marchive.getInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mzae[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m502[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;35mFiles.copy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, target[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m503[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAnalysis and Root Cause:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The fuzzer trace after the last patch shows the path‐traversal is still [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtriggered in the ZIP‐specific branch of `Expander.expand` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m490[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m503[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, not in [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe generic loop we already patched.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. That branch uses:[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Path target = [0m[1;35mtargetDirectory.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mzae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mtarget.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirectory[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m … throw; [0m[1;39m}[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Path parent = [0m[1;35mcreateParentDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirectory, target[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   …[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;35mFiles.copy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, target[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Despite the initial `startsWith` check, a clever entry name can subvert the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparent‐directory creation logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39min `createParentDirectory`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to point outside the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintended target directory before the `Files.copy` call—thus triggering Jazzer’s [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msanitizer.  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. In short, while the normalized target path is validated, the subsequent[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   `createParentDirectory` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich likely does its own resolve/normalize logic and [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcreates intermediate directories[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m can reintroduce a path outside `targetDirectory`.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mStrategy to Fix:[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. General Principle: Any time we resolve an entry name against `targetDirectory`, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore performing I/O [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdirectory creation or file write/copy[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, we must:[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Resolve and normalize the full path;  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Convert to an absolute path;  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Assert that it begins with the absolute, normalized `targetDirectory`;  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Only then proceed to create parents or write files.  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Steps to Implement Patch:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Factor out a helper in `Expander.java`, e.g.,  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      private Path [0m[1;35msafeResolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath baseDir, String entryName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          Path raw = [0m[1;35mbaseDir.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mentryName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          Path absNorm = [0m[1;35mraw.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          Path baseAbsNorm = [0m[1;35mbaseDir.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mabsNorm.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbaseAbsNorm[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"File path traversal: '"[0m[39m + baseAbsNorm + [0m[32m"' -> [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m'"[0m[39m + absNorm + [0m[32m"'"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          return absNorm;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. In the ZIP‐specific branch, replace:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      Path target = [0m[1;35mtargetDirectory.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mzae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mtarget.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirectory[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m … [0m[1;39m}[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      Path parent = [0m[1;35mcreateParentDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirectory, target[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      …[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;35mFiles.copy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, target[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      with:[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      Path absTarget = [0m[1;35msafeResolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirectory, [0m[1;35mzae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      Path parent = [0m[1;35mabsTarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Failed to create directory "[0m[39m + parent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream is = [0m[1;35marchive.getInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mzae[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mFiles.copy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, absTarget[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Similarly, in any other specialized branches [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., Tar, Cpio, 7z[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, call [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`safeResolve` before any directory or file I/O.  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Remove or retire the old `createParentDirectory` helper if it cannot be [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbrought into compliance; or refactor it to leverage `safeResolve` internally, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensuring double‐checks on the absolute, normalized path.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Preserve Existing Logic:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The new `safeResolve` enforces the same normalization and `startsWith` check [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwe already applied in the generic loop, but stronger—using absolute paths to [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprevent bypass via relative base dirs.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We create parents immediately on the validated, absolute path rather than [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtrying to correct mismatches afterward.  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Mitigating Side Effects:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Converting to absolute paths will not affect valid entries, since [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mabsolute[0m[1;39m([0m[39m`baseDir/entry`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m of a relative base plus a relative entry yields the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrect on‐filesystem path.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Tests or users that relied on the old behavior [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., trusting [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`createParentDirectory` to create multiple nested levels[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m should see no change: [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectories will still be created.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The check is purely preventative—no legitimate extraction will be blocked.  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Similar Code Patterns:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The generic loop patch around line [0m[1;36m71[0m[39m should be consolidated to use [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`safeResolve` as well.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing ZIP‐slip mitigations [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe original `[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` + `startsWith`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbecome redundant and can be replaced with the one‐line `safeResolve` call for [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconsistency and to cover both path and parent creation.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWith this unified approach, every path operation is guarded by an absolute‐path, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnormalized `startsWith` check, fully mitigating traversal exploits flagged by [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJazzer.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m. Initial Issue                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - A Jazzer crash log reports:                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              ```                                                                            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m            - The fuzzer identifies that during archive expansion, an entry name containing  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         path segments [1m([0m`..[35m/[0m` or absolute paths[1m)[0m leads to a                                  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         extraction root.                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Jazzer’s `FilePathTraversal` sanitizer raises a security issue when an output  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         path falls outside the permitted base directory.                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m. Patch Attempt                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - In `Expander.java`, the code handling non-directory entries was modified:      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              - Renamed `target` to `absTarget` and computed it as                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                `[1;35mtargetDirectory.toAbsolutePath[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1;35m.resolve[0m[1m([0m[1;35mzae.getName[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1m)[0m[1;35m.normali[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mze[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`.                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              - Introduced `baseAbsNorm` as the normalized absolute path of                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `targetDirectory`.                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              - Added a check: if `![1;35mabsTarget.startsWith[0m[1m([0mbaseAbsNorm[1m)[0m`, throw                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[1;35mIOException[0m[1m([0m[32m"File path traversal..."[0m[1m)[0m`.                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              - Simplified parent directory creation: use `[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1m([0mparent[1m)[0m`  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         on `[1;35mabsTarget.getParent[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`.                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              - Updated the copy call to `[1;35mFiles.copy[0m[1m([0mis, absTarget[1m)[0m`.                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The diff context [1m([0mlines ~[1;36m488[0m–[1;36m506[0m[1m)[0m clarifies the replacement of the old         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         zip-slip guard and the new absolute-path approach.                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Jazzer fuzz run on the Apache Commons Compress Expander example triggered a [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` exception for file path traversal. In response, a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpatch was proposed that introduces `[0m[1;35mtoAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mstartsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbaseAbsNorm[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` checks around directory creation, symbolic‐link handling,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand file extraction to block paths that escape the target directory. After applying[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe patch, the build fails with a cascade of compilation errors—primarily “else [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout if” and “class, interface, or enum expected”—indicating unbalanced or [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmisplaced braces in `Expander.java`.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInitial issue  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• A fuzz test [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m feeds crafted archives into [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Expander.expand`.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• Jazzer’s `FilePathTraversal.check` sanitizer throws a critical exception on [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/tmp/.../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m`, reporting a path that escapes the intended output [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectory.  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• Stack trace points to multiple overloads of `Expander.expand` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m216[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m336[0m[39m, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m412[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m502[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m before hitting the fuzzer harness.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mImportant observations  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• The vulnerability is a classic zip‐slip/path traversal: entries in the archive [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcan resolve to locations outside the designated output directory.  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• The exception is thrown by Jazzer’s built‐in sanitizer, not by any explicit check[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min Commons Compress.  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• There are three extraction paths in `Expander.expand`: directory entries, Unix [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msymlinks, and regular file entries—each must be hardened.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch attempt  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. At the top of the loop over `nextEntry`, for directory entries:  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Compute `baseAbsNorm = [0m[1;35mtargetDirPath.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Compute `absTargetPath = [0m[1;35mtargetPath.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If `![0m[1;35mabsTargetPath.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbaseAbsNorm[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, throw `[0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"File path [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mtraversal: ..."[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Proceed to create directories on the normalized path.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. In the Unix‐symlink branch [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mzae.isUnixSymlink[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Normalize and check both the link location [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`absLink`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and the symlink target [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`absTarget`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m against `baseAbsNorm`.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Create missing parent directories.  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Use `[0m[1;35mFiles.createSymbolicLink[0m[1;39m([0m[39mabsLink, [0m[1;35mbaseAbsNorm.relativize[0m[1;39m([0m[39mabsTarget[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39monly if `absLink` does not yet exist.  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. In the regular‐file branch:  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Normalize and check the resolved file path [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`absTarget`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m against [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`baseAbsNorm`.  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Create parent directories if needed.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Copy the entry’s data via `[0m[1;35mFiles.copy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, absTarget[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch‐result log  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• Maven reports [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m errors in `Expander.java`, starting with “‘else’ without ‘if’” [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mat line [0m[1;36m504[0m[39m, then a series of “class, interface, or enum expected” errors.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• These errors point to unbalanced or misplaced braces surrounding the newly [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minserted code blocks, causing the Java parser to lose track of method and class [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mboundaries.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
