[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m76[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!nullTarget && ![0m[1;35mFiles.isDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m77[0m[39m:                    throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Failed to create directory "[0m[39m + [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtargetPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m78[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m79[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m80[0m[39m:                final Path parent = nullTarget ? null : [0m[1;35mtargetPath.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m81[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!nullTarget && ![0m[1;35mFiles.isDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m82[0m[39m:                    throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Failed to create directory "[0m[39m + [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m83[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m84[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnullTarget[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m85[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;35mwriter.accept[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnextEntry, NullOutputStream.INSTANCE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m86[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m87[0m[39m:                    try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOutputStream outputStream = [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mFiles.newOutputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m88[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;35mwriter.accept[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnextEntry, outputStream[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m89[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m90[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m91[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m92[0m[39m:            nextEntry = [0m[1;35msupplier.get[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m93[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m94[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The compilation failures stem from unbalanced or misplaced braces in the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mZipArchive‐based `expand` method after inserting the normalization and traversal [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchecks. The existing code uses a two‐branch structure [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35misUnixSymlink[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m … [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39melse if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35misDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m … [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m but does not explicitly handle directory entries, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleading to overly complex nesting when we try to inject safeguarding logic. We will[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msimplify and harden this method by restructuring it into a clear three‐branch [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`if/else if/else`—one branch each for symlinks, directories, and regular [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfiles—ensuring every `[0m[1;39m{[0m[39m` has a matching `[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` and that no stray braces remain.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Detailed Steps  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Locate the ZipArchive loop in `Expander.java` around line ~[0m[1;36m475[0m[39m:[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      while [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mentries.hasMoreElements[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ZipArchiveEntry zae = [0m[1;35mentries.nextElement[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m currently: if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35misUnixSymlink[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m … [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35misDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m … [0m[1;39m}[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[33m...[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Replace that two‐branch structure with an explicit three‐branch structure:[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      while [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mentries.hasMoreElements[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ZipArchiveEntry zae = [0m[1;35mentries.nextElement[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Unix symlink entries[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mzae.isUnixSymlink[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Normalize base directory[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mii[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Compute and normalize the link path[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39miii[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Check [0m[1;35mstartsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbase[0m[1;39m)[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39miv[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m mkdirs on link parent if needed[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mv[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Compute and normalize the target of the link[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvi[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Check [0m[1;35mstartsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbase[0m[1;39m)[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvii[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m createSymbolicLink if absent[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Explicit directory entries[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          else if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mzae.isDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Normalize base directory[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mii[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Compute and normalize the directory path[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39miii[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Check [0m[1;35mstartsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbase[0m[1;39m)[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39miv[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Files.createDirectories on that path[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m3[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Regular file entries[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Normalize base directory[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mii[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Compute and normalize the file path[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39miii[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Check [0m[1;35mstartsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbase[0m[1;39m)[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39miv[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Ensure parent directories exist via [0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mv[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Copy data via [0m[1;35mFiles.copy[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. In each branch:  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – Call `Path baseAbsNorm = [0m[1;35mtargetDirectory.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39monce per iteration to avoid repetition.  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – Resolve and normalize the entry path against `baseAbsNorm`.  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – Immediately throw `[0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"File path traversal: ..."[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` if [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`![0m[1;35mresolvedPath.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbaseAbsNorm[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – Use `[0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnot the older `createParentDirectory`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto create any missing directories.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – For symlinks, use `[0m[1;35mFiles.createSymbolicLink[0m[1;39m([0m[39mabsLink, [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mbaseAbsNorm.relativize[0m[1;39m([0m[39mabsTarget[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Brace Alignment  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Each `if` and `else if` and final `else` has exactly one opening `[0m[1;39m{[0m[39m` and one [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclosing `[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m`.  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The loop itself has its own `[0m[1;39m{[0m[39m … [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m`.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No nested `else` or stray braces remain.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Preserve Existing Functionality  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The generic `[0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mArchiveEntrySupplier, ArchiveEntryBiConsumer, Path[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverload remains unchanged beyond its own directory‐branch normalization patch [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mwhich already compiles[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Test harnesses, utility methods [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`createParentDirectory`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and fuzzing logic [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mare untouched.  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We retain the original semantic: symlinks first, directories second, files [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlast.  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A three‐branch `if/else if/else` is easier to reason about and less prone to [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbrace‐mismatch than injecting extra checks into an existing two‐branch model.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Normalization and `startsWith` checks in all three branches effectively block [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mzip‐slip/path traversal.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Explicitly handling directories in the ZipArchive method mirrors the generic [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverload’s approach and prevents silent skipping of directory entries.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Using `[0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` ensures parent directories are created in[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mone call.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigations  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Performance overhead: trivial [0m[1;39m([0m[39mone extra `[0m[1;35mtoAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` per [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentry[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Behavior: directory entries will now throw an exception if they traverse [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moutside `targetDirectory`; this is intended.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensure tests expecting the original create‐directory behavior still pass [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthey[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwill, since we only add security checks[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
